    SELECT [o0].[Id], [o0].[OrderId], [m].[Id] AS [Id0], [c].[Id] AS [Id1]
    FROM [OrdersDetails] AS [o0]
    LEFT JOIN [MenuSalesItems] AS [m] ON [o0].[MenuSalesItemId] = [m].[Id]

) AS [t] ON [o].[Id] = [t].[OrderId]
